                          <div class="UDZeY fAgajc OTFaAf">
                           <div class="wDYxhc" data-hveid="CDYQAA" data-md="50" data-ved="2ahUKEwjUwsn89-31AhUXkYkEHUA8CrMQkCl6BAg2EAA" lang="en-US" style="clear:none">
                            <div class="PZPZlf hb8SAc" data-attrid="description" data-hveid="CDYQAQ" data-ved="2ahUKEwjUwsn89-31AhUXkYkEHUA8CrMQziAoAHoECDYQAQ">
                             <div jsaction="SKAaMe:c0XUbe;rcuQ6b:npT2md" jscontroller="GCSbhd">
                              <div jsaction="rcuQ6b:npT2md" jscontroller="QhoyLd">
                               <div class="kno-rdesc" jsaction="seM7Qe:c0XUbe;Iigoee:c0XUbe;rcuQ6b:npT2md" jscontroller="GCSbhd" jsname="g7W7Ed">
                                <span>
                                 A kitten is a juvenile cat. After being born, kittens display primary altriciality and are totally dependent on their mothers for survival. They normally do not open their eyes for seven to ten days. After about two weeks, kittens develop quickly and begin to explore the world outside their nest.
                                </span>
